<user_id>101841350963225198956<//user_id><username>Benjamin Oldenburg</username><time>1563831428760<//time><Rate>1< /Rate>< review>
Do not use this service.  I decided to read the other reviews to see if anyone had a similar experience. I noticed that for any negative review their response was "1 JOB LANDED US 12 BAD REVIEWS FROM FRIENDS"

It's not impossible but pretty farfetched to believe that someone got 11 other friends to join them in review bombing some low tiered tow company. Especially when you look at the reviews and they're all posted at completely different times, some even months apart.

So what that tells me is that these negative reviews have been earned by the tow company itself and not some conspiracy amongst friends.

That being said if you feel like making your bad day even worse then this is definitely the company to waste your time, energy, and money with. Otherwise, you're better off going with literally any other tow company.</review>

< text>
This UPS location is very efficient for mailing packages as well as drop-offs. Because they are so quick, there is usually no line when I come in. Once in a while there, I have to wait and am the only person in line. But it's only for a a minute or so because they have lots of staff and multiple weigh stations for packages. A way better experience than the US Post Office.

The biggest issue here is the parking situation on Castro. There is a limited supply of street parking for a multitude of businesses. Save yourself a headache and forget coming at lunch time during the week. Other times it's hit or miss, and it's not fun carrying boxes of stuff for any long distance so good luck there.

That said, there's a Starbucks nearby, so anytime I have to work carrying a package, I can treat myself do a drink there.< /text>

< review>
I go to this location often.  I do field service, and I am always sending back defective networking devices I have replaced.  The staff is fast, polite and efficient.  I don't expect them to supply packing tape for me, becuase if they did that, they would supply it for everyone that walked in the door.  For that reason, I arrive there with my package taped up and labeled, if I have a label. If not, they have no trouble generating a label for me, based on the business I am shipping to.  If their account doesn't come up, or there are issues with the account, I simply recall that this is not UPS's problem, it's the problem of the person or business that wants their stuff back, so I would not even think of yelling at the staff about this...they can, and do, however, answer questions for me.
Great location...the only issus is trying to find  parking in downtown Mountain View...eh...that's the price we pay for convenience.  Keep it up, #120 staff!</review>

<Pics>None< /Pics>< review>
Lance Cabo 200i
I've been wanting a scooter for several years. I finally made it down to Scooter City last year because they are the only Lance dealers nearby. I've been wanting to check one out in person because a picture obviously isn't the same. I was feeling the dread of walking into a "dealership" expecting rude people with hard sales; however, I was immediately correctly and pleasantly surprised. The individual was incredibly nice and informative. He explained manufacturing backgrounds between the brands and follow up maintenance records. After hearing what I wanted, he gave me a brochure with some other websites. He suggested I look into a few other comparable options before making a final decision. No hard sales. I continued on with my life and went through the process of getting a motorcycle license. I came back 6-7 months later and experienced the exact same informative kindness. I bought a Lance that was already in the shop and took it home that evening. Very nice people that aren't pushy. They're knowledgeable willing to share that knowledge. Its obvious this is their passion. Great experience overall.< /review>

< Pictures>
None< /Pictures>
<text>The guy that helped me with an acoustic and an electric setup was friendly. Both guitars are in much better shape.

My fender hellcat acoustic had action that was way too high. It's much easier to play after he lowered the bridge, strung up some new strings and adjusted the truss rod. Sustain is improved on higher frets as well since it's way easier to push down the strings. Super happy with this setup.

My Ibanez gio seemed impossible to intonate the g string when I left it and the action was set high to compensate for the last 4 frets not ringing out at all. He straightened out the truss rod, replaced the strings and lowered the action. Sustain is improved across the whole fretboard and the intonation seems to be fixed. There's still slight buzzing when I play hard, but it's a cheap electric and I wasn't expecting there not to be. Probably needs a little fretwork. For $50 bucks the other fixes made it worthwhile.

I'm happy with both setups. Best $110 I ever spent.< /text>< Rating>
5< /Rating>
